Step 4.2: Create Main Go Application
bash
cat > main.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
    "context"
    "log"
    "net/http"
    "net/http/httputil"
    "net/url"
    "os"
    "os/signal"
    "syscall"
    "time"

    "github.com/gin-gonic/gin"
    "github.com/gorilla/websocket"
    "github.com/ulule/limiter/v3"
    "github.com/ulule/limiter/v3/drivers/store/memory"
)

var upgrader = websocket.Upgrader{
    CheckOrigin: func(r *http.Request) bool { return true },
}

type Hub struct {
    clients    map[*Client]bool
    broadcast  chan []byte
    register   chan *Client
    unregister chan *Client
}

type Client struct {
    hub  *Hub
    conn *websocket.Conn
    send chan []byte
    id   string
}

func newHub() *Hub {
    return &Hub{
        clients:    make(map[*Client]bool),
        broadcast:  make(chan []byte),
        register:   make(chan *Client),
        unregister: make(chan *Client),
    }
}

func (h *Hub) run() {
    for {
        select {
        case client := <-h.register:
            h.clients[client] = true
            log.Printf("Client %s connected. Total clients: %d", client.id, len(h.clients))
        case client := <-h.unregister:
            if _, ok := h.clients[client]; ok {
                delete(h.clients, client)
                close(client.send)
                log.Printf("Client %s disconnected. Total clients: %d", client.id, len(h.clients))
            }
        case message := <-h.broadcast:
            for client := range h.clients {
                select {
                case client.send <- message:
                default:
                    close(client.send)
                    delete(h.clients, client)
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

func (c *Client) writePump() {
    ticker := time.NewTicker(30 * time.Second)
    defer func() {
        ticker.Stop()
        c.conn.Close()
    }()
    for {
        select {
        case message, ok := <-c.send:
            if !ok {
                c.conn.WriteMessage(websocket.CloseMessage, []byte{})
                return
            }
            c.conn.WriteMessage(websocket.TextMessage, message)
        case <-ticker.C:
            c.conn.WriteMessage(websocket.PingMessage, nil)
        }
    }
}

func (c *Client) readPump() {
    defer func() {
        c.hub.unregister <- c
        c.conn.Close()
    }()
    for {
        _, message, err := c.conn.ReadMessage()
        if err != nil {
            break
        }
        c.hub.broadcast <- message
    }
}

func serveWs(hub *Hub, c *gin.Context) {
    conn, err := upgrader.Upgrade(c.Writer, c.Request, nil)
    if err != nil {
        log.Printf("WebSocket upgrade failed: %v", err)
        return
    }
    clientID := c.Query("client_id")
    if clientID == "" {
        clientID = "anonymous"
    }
    client := &Client{
        hub:  hub,
        conn: conn,
        send: make(chan []byte, 256),
        id:   clientID,
    }
    client.hub.register <- client
    go client.writePump()
    go client.readPump()
}

type Server struct {
    router       *gin.Engine
    hub          *Hub
    rateLimiter  *limiter.Limiter
    orchestrator *url.URL
}

func NewServer(orchestratorURL string) *Server {
    rate, _ := limiter.NewRateFromFormatted("100-M")
    store := memory.NewStore()
    
    orchURL, _ := url.Parse(orchestratorURL)
    
    s := &Server{
        router:       gin.Default(),
        hub:          newHub(),
        rateLimiter:  limiter.New(store, rate),
        orchestrator: orchURL,
    }
    
    s.setupRoutes()
    return s
}

func (s *Server) setupRoutes() {
    s.router.GET("/health", func(c *gin.Context) {
        c.JSON(200, gin.H{"status": "ok", "clients": len(s.hub.clients)})
    })
    
    s.router.GET("/ws", func(c *gin.Context) {
        serveWs(s.hub, c)
    })
    
    s.router.POST("/broadcast", func(c *gin.Context) {
        var msg struct {
            Message string `json:"message"`
        }
        if err := c.ShouldBindJSON(&msg); err == nil {
            s.hub.broadcast <- []byte(msg.Message)
            c.JSON(200, gin.H{"status": "broadcast"})
        } else {
            c.JSON(400, gin.H{"error": "invalid request"})
        }
    })
    
    // Proxy all other requests to orchestrator
    s.router.Any("/api/*path", s.rateLimitMiddleware(), s.proxyToOrchestrator)
}

func (s *Server) proxyToOrchestrator(c *gin.Context) {
    proxy := httputil.NewSingleHostReverseProxy(s.orchestrator)
    proxy.ServeHTTP(c.Writer, c.Request)
}

func (s *Server) rateLimitMiddleware() gin.HandlerFunc {
    return func(c *gin.Context) {
        ctx := context.Background()
        key := c.ClientIP()
        
        limiterCtx, err := s.rateLimiter.Get(ctx, key)
        if err != nil {
            c.Next()
            return
        }
        
        if limiterCtx.Reached {
            c.JSON(429, gin.H{"error": "rate limit exceeded"})
            c.Abort()
            return
        }
        
        c.Next()
    }
}

func main() {
    orchestratorURL := os.Getenv("ORCHESTRATOR_URL")
    if orchestratorURL == "" {
        orchestratorURL = "http://localhost:8000"
    }
    
    server := NewServer(orchestratorURL)
    go server.hub.run()
    
    srv := &http.Server{
        Addr:    ":3000",
        Handler: server.router,
    }
    
    go func() {
        if err := srv.ListenAndServe(); err != nil && err != http.ErrServerClosed {
            log.Fatalf("listen: %s", err)
        }
    }()
    
    log.Println("🚀 Gateway running on :3000")
    log.Printf("📡 WebSocket endpoint: ws://localhost:3000/ws")
    log.Printf("🔄 Proxying to orchestrator: %s", orchestratorURL)
    
    quit := make(chan os.Signal, 1)
    signal.Notify(quit, syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM)
    <-quit
    
    log.Println("Shutting down server...")
    ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 5*time.Second)
    defer cancel()
    
    if err := srv.Shutdown(ctx); err != nil {
        log.Fatal("Server forced to shutdown:", err)
    }
    
    log.Println("Server exited")
}
EOF

import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:flutter_riverpod/flutter_riverpod.dart';
import 'package:finos_app/routing/app_router.dart';
import 'package:finos_app/theme/app_theme.dart';

void main() {
  runApp(const ProviderScope(child: FinOSApp()));
}

class FinOSApp extends ConsumerWidget {
  const FinOSApp({super.key});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context, WidgetRef ref) {
    final router = ref.watch(appRouterProvider);
    
    return MaterialApp.router(
      title: 'Financial OS',
      theme: AppTheme.darkTheme,
      routerConfig: router,
      debugShowCheckedModeBanner: false,
    );
  }
}

Step 5.5: Create Router
bash
mkdir -p lib/routing
cat > lib/routing/app_router.dart << 'EOF'
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:go_router/go_router.dart';
import 'package:flutter_riverpod/flutter_riverpod.dart';
import 'package:finos_app/screens/dashboard.dart';
import 'package:finos_app/screens/portfolio.dart';
import 'package:finos_app/screens/trading.dart';
import 'package:finos_app/screens/settings.dart';

final appRouterProvider = Provider<GoRouter>((ref) {
  return GoRouter(
    initialLocation: '/dashboard',
    routes: [
      ShellRoute(
        builder: (context, state, child) {
          return ScaffoldWithNavBar(child: child);
        },
        routes: [
          GoRoute(
            path: '/dashboard',
            builder: (context, state) => const Dashboard(),
          ),
          GoRoute(
            path: '/portfolio',
            builder: (context, state) => const Portfolio(),
          ),
          GoRoute(
            path: '/trading',
            builder: (context, state) => const Trading(),
          ),
          GoRoute(
            path: '/settings',
            builder: (context, state) => const Settings(),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    ],
  );
});

class ScaffoldWithNavBar extends StatelessWidget {
  final Widget child;
  const ScaffoldWithNavBar({super.key, required this.child});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: child,
      bottomNavigationBar: NavigationBar(
        destinations: const [
          NavigationDestination(icon: Icon(Icons.dashboard), label: 'Dashboard'),
          NavigationDestination(icon: Icon(Icons.pie_chart), label: 'Portfolio'),
          NavigationDestination(icon: Icon(Icons.swap_horiz), label: 'Trading'),
          NavigationDestination(icon: Icon(Icons.settings), label: 'Settings'),
        ],
        onDestinationSelected: (index) {
          switch (index) {
            case 0: context.go('/dashboard'); break;
            case 1: context.go('/portfolio'); break;
            case 2: context.go('/trading'); break;
            case 3: context.go('/settings'); break;
          }
        },
      ),
    );
  }
}

import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:flutter_riverpod/flutter_riverpod.dart';
import 'package:finos_app/providers/portfolio_provider.dart';
import 'package:fl_chart/fl_chart.dart';

class Dashboard extends ConsumerStatefulWidget {
  const Dashboard({super.key});

  @override
  ConsumerState<Dashboard> createState() => _DashboardState();
}

class _DashboardState extends ConsumerState<Dashboard> {
  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    Future.microtask(() => ref.read(portfolioProvider.notifier).fetchPortfolio());
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final portfolio = ref.watch(portfolioProvider);
    
    return Scaffold(
      appBar: AppBar(
        title: const Text('Financial OS'),
        actions: [
          IconButton(
            icon: const Icon(Icons.refresh),
            onPressed: () => ref.read(portfolioProvider.notifier).fetchPortfolio(),
          ),
        ],
      ),
      body: portfolio.when(
        data: (data) => ListView(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
          children: [
            Card(
              child: Padding(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
                child: Column(
                  crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                  children: [
                    Text('Net Worth', style: Theme.of(context).textTheme.titleMedium),
                    const SizedBox(height: 8),
                    Text(
                      '£${data.totalValue.toStringAsFixed(2)}',
                      style: Theme.of(context).textTheme.displaySmall,
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(height: 8),
                    Row(
                      children: [
                        _ChangeChip(value: data.dailyChange, label: 'Today'),
                        const SizedBox(width: 12),
                        _ChangeChip(value: data.totalReturn, label: 'Total'),
                      ],
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 16),
            Card(
              child: Padding(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
                child: Column(
                  crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                  children: [
                    Text('Asset Allocation', style: Theme.of(context).textTheme.titleMedium),
                    const SizedBox(height: 16),
                    SizedBox(
                      height: 200,
                      child: PieChart(
                        PieChartData(
                          sections: _buildSections(data.allocation),
                          centerSpaceRadius: 40,
                        ),
                      ),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        loading: () => const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator()),
        error: (err, _) => Center(child: Text('Error: $err')),
      ),
    );
  }

  List<PieChartSectionData> _buildSections(Map<String, double> allocation) {
    final colors = [Colors.blue, Colors.green, Colors.orange, Colors.purple, Colors.red];
    return allocation.entries.map((entry) {
      final index = allocation.keys.toList().indexOf(entry.key);
      return PieChartSectionData(
        value: entry.value,
        title: '${entry.key}\n${entry.value.toStringAsFixed(1)}%',
        color: colors[index % colors.length],
        radius: 50,
        titleStyle: const TextStyle(fontSize: 12, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold),
      );
    }).toList();
  }
}

class _ChangeChip extends StatelessWidget {
  final double value;
  final String label;
  const _ChangeChip({required this.value, required this.label});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final isPositive = value >= 0;
    return Chip(
      avatar: Icon(isPositive ? Icons.trending_up : Icons.trending_down, size: 16),
      label: Text('$label: ${isPositive ? '+' : ''}${value.toStringAsFixed(2)}%'),
      backgroundColor: isPositive ? Colors.green.shade900 : Colors.red.shade900,
    );
  }
}

Step 5.7: Create Providers
bash
mkdir -p lib/providers
cat > lib/providers/portfolio_provider.dart << 'EOF'
import 'package:dio/dio.dart';
import 'package:flutter_riverpod/flutter_riverpod.dart';
import 'package:freezed_annotation/freezed_annotation.dart';
import 'package:finos_app/models/portfolio.dart';

part 'portfolio_provider.freezed.dart';

final portfolioProvider = StateNotifierProvider<PortfolioNotifier, AsyncValue<PortfolioData>>((ref) {
  return PortfolioNotifier();
});

class PortfolioNotifier extends StateNotifier<AsyncValue<PortfolioData>> {
  PortfolioNotifier() : super(const AsyncValue.loading());
  final _dio = Dio(BaseOptions(baseUrl: 'http://localhost:3000'));

  Future<void> fetchPortfolio() async {
    try {
      final response = await _dio.get('/api/portfolio/summary');
      final data = PortfolioData.fromJson(response.data);
      state = AsyncValue.data(data);
    } catch (e, st) {
      state = AsyncValue.error(e, st);
    }
  }
}

@freezed
class PortfolioData with _$PortfolioData {
  const factory PortfolioData({
    required double totalValue,
    @Default(0.0) double dailyChange,
    @Default(0.0) double totalReturn,
    @Default({}) Map<String, double> allocation,
    @Default([]) List<Holding> holdings,
  }) = _PortfolioData;

  factory PortfolioData.fromJson(Map<String, dynamic> json) {
    return PortfolioData(
      totalValue: (json['total_value'] as num?)?.toDouble() ?? 0.0,
      dailyChange: (json['daily_return'] as num?)?.toDouble() ?? 0.0,
      totalReturn: (json['total_return'] as num?)?.toDouble() ?? 0.0,
      allocation: _calculateAllocation(json['holdings'] as List? ?? []),
      holdings: (json['holdings'] as List?)?.map((h) => Holding.fromJson(h)).toList() ?? [],
    );
  }

  static Map<String, double> _calculateAllocation(List<dynamic> holdings) {
    final Map<String, double> allocation = {};
    double total = 0;
    for (var h in holdings) {
      total += (h['current_value'] as num?)?.toDouble() ?? 0.0;
    }
    if (total == 0) return {};
    for (var h in holdings) {
      final type = h['asset_type'] ?? 'other';
      final value = (h['current_value'] as num?)?.toDouble() ?? 0.0;
      allocation[type] = (allocation[type] ?? 0) + (value / total * 100);
    }
    return allocation;
  }
}
EOF

Step 7.3: Set Up Automated Encrypted Backups
bash
cat > ~/finos/backup.sh << 'EOF'
#!/bin/bash
set -e
DATE=$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S)
BACKUP_DIR="/home/finos/backups"
mkdir -p "$BACKUP_DIR"

echo "🔒 Stopping services for consistent backup..."
cd ~/finos
docker-compose down

echo "📦 Creating encrypted backup..."
sudo tar -czf - ~/finos 2>/dev/null | openssl enc -aes-256-cbc -pbkdf2 -salt -pass pass:"${BACKUP_PASSPHRASE:-changeme}" -out "$BACKUP_DIR/finos-$DATE.tar.gz.enc"

echo "🚀 Restarting services..."
docker-compose up -d

echo "🗑️ Removing backups older than 30 days..."
find "$BACKUP_DIR" -type f -mtime +30 -delete

echo "✅ Backup complete: finos-$DATE.tar.gz.enc"
EOF

chmod +x ~/finos/backup.sh

# Schedule daily backup at 2 AM
(crontab -l 2>/dev/null; echo "0 2 * * * /home/finos/finos/backup.sh >> /home/finos/backups/backup.log 2>&1") | crontab -

3.2 The Session-Aware Orchestrator
python
# orchestrator/session_aware_router.py
from enum import Enum
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from typing import Optional

class TradingSession(Enum):
    SYDNEY = "sydney"
    TOKYO = "tokyo"
    LONDON = "london"
    NEW_YORK = "new_york"
    OVERLAP_LONDON_NY = "overlap_ln"
    WEEKEND = "weekend"

class SessionAwareRouter:
    def __init__(self):
        self.session_strategies = {
            TradingSession.SYDNEY: ["forex_aud_jpy", "crypto_perps", "defi_yield"],
            TradingSession.TOKYO: ["forex_usd_jpy", "nikkei_futures", "crypto_arbitrage"],
            TradingSession.LONDON: ["forex_eur_usd", "ftse_perps", "gold_perps"],
            TradingSession.NEW_YORK: ["us_equity_perps", "cme_futures", "forex_usd"],
            TradingSession.OVERLAP_LONDON_NY: ["all_forex_majors", "crypto_perps"],
            TradingSession.WEEKEND: ["crypto_perps", "defi_farming", "staking", "ecommerce"],
        }
    
    def get_current_session(self) -> TradingSession:
        now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
        hour = now.hour
        weekday = now.weekday()
        
        if weekday >= 5:  # Saturday or Sunday
            return TradingSession.WEEKEND
        
        if 21 <= hour or hour < 6:
            return TradingSession.SYDNEY
        elif 0 <= hour < 9:
            return TradingSession.TOKYO
        elif 7 <= hour < 16:
            return TradingSession.LONDON if 13 <= hour < 16 else TradingSession.OVERLAP_LONDON_NY
        elif 13 <= hour < 22:
            return TradingSession.NEW_YORK
        else:
            return TradingSession.WEEKEND
    
    def get_active_strategies(self) -> list:
        session = self.get_current_session()
        return self.session_strategies[session]
    
    def route_capital(self, available_capital: float) -> dict:
        strategies = self.get_active_strategies()
        allocation = {}
        weights = self._calculate_weights(strategies)
        for strategy, weight in weights.items():
            allocation[strategy] = available_capital * weight
        return allocation

4.2 Flutter Responsive Architecture
dart
// lib/utils/responsive.dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class Responsive {
  static bool isMobile(BuildContext context) =>
      MediaQuery.of(context).size.width < 650;
  
  static bool isTablet(BuildContext context) =>
      MediaQuery.of(context).size.width >= 650 &&
      MediaQuery.of(context).size.width < 1100;
  
  static bool isDesktop(BuildContext context) =>
      MediaQuery.of(context).size.width >= 1100;
  
  static T value<T>(BuildContext context, {
    required T mobile,
    T? tablet,
    T? desktop,
  }) {
    if (isDesktop(context) && desktop != null) return desktop;
    if (isTablet(context) && tablet != null) return tablet;
    return mobile;
  }
}

// lib/screens/dashboard.dart
class Dashboard extends StatelessWidget {
  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: Responsive.value(
        context,
        mobile: _MobileDashboard(),
        tablet: _TabletDashboard(),
        desktop: _DesktopDashboard(),
      ),
    );
  }
}
4.3 Real-Time Sync Across All Devices
dart
// lib/services/sync_service.dart
import 'package:web_socket_channel/web_socket_channel.dart';
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';

class SyncService {
  static final SyncService _instance = SyncService._internal();
  factory SyncService() => _instance;
  SyncService._internal();
  
  WebSocketChannel? _channel;
  final Map<String, dynamic> _localCache = {};
  
  void connect(String serverUrl) {
    _channel = WebSocketChannel.connect(Uri.parse(serverUrl));
    _channel!.stream.listen((message) {
      final data = jsonDecode(message);
      _localCache[data['key']] = data['value'];
      _notifyListeners(data['key']);
    });
  }
  
  Future<void> syncOfflineData() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    final offlineChanges = prefs.getStringList('offline_changes') ?? [];
    for (final change in offlineChanges) {
      _channel!.sink.add(change);
    }
    await prefs.remove('offline_changes');
  }
  
  void _notifyListeners(String key) {
    // Riverpod state update
  }
}

🤖 Part 1: The Autopilot Opportunity Scanner

1.1 The Opportunity Scanner Architecture
python
# orchestrator/opportunity_scanner.py
from enum import Enum
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Dict, Optional
import duckdb
from datetime import datetime

class CapitalTier(Enum):
    MICRO = "micro"      # £1 - £500
    SMALL = "small"      # £500 - £5,000
    MEDIUM = "medium"    # £5,000 - £50,000
    HIGH = "high"        # £50,000+

class TimeHorizon(Enum):
    IMMEDIATE = "immediate"  # < 24 hours
    SHORT = "short"          # 1-30 days
    MEDIUM = "medium"        # 1-12 months
    LONG = "long"            # 1+ years

@dataclass
class Opportunity:
    name: str
    category: str
    platform: str
    min_capital: float
    expected_return: str
    risk_level: str
    time_horizon: TimeHorizon
    automation_level: str
    active_hours: Optional[str] = "24/7"

class OpportunityScanner:
    def __init__(self, duckdb_conn):
        self.conn = duckdb_conn
        
    def scan_opportunities(
        self, 
        available_capital: float, 
        tier: CapitalTier,
        preferred_time_horizon: Optional[TimeHorizon] = None,
        max_risk: Optional[str] = None
    ) -> List[Opportunity]:
        """Scan the financial master database for matching opportunities."""
        query = """
        SELECT * FROM opportunities 
        WHERE min_capital <= ? 
        AND (risk_level <= ? OR ? IS NULL)
        ORDER BY expected_return DESC
        """
        # In production, this queries your DuckDB/PostgreSQL opportunity database
        results = self.conn.execute(query, [
            available_capital, 
            max_risk or 'high', 
            max_risk
        ]).fetchdf()
        
        return [Opportunity(**row) for row in results.to_dict('records')]
    
    def auto_allocate(self, capital: float) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Automatically allocate capital across the best opportunities."""
        opportunities = self.scan_opportunities(capital, CapitalTier.MICRO)
        allocation = {}
        remaining = capital
        
        # Smart allocation algorithm
        for opp in opportunities[:5]:  # Top 5 opportunities
            if opp.min_capital <= remaining:
                # Allocate based on risk-adjusted return
                weight = self._calculate_weight(opp)
                alloc = min(remaining * weight, remaining)
                allocation[opp.name] = alloc
                remaining -= alloc
        
        return allocation

1% Rule (Risk Management)	Never risk > 1% of capital per trade	Active trading	Active trading enabled
4% Rule (Safe Withdrawal)	Withdraw 4% annually in retirement	Retirement planning	Age > 50; retirement horizon

All-Weather Portfolio	Equal risk across economic environments	Inflation/volatility protection	High inflation environment

🧠 Part 2: The Intelligent Rule Engine
Your system will dynamically select and apply the optimal rule based on real-time analysis of your financial state.

python
# orchestrator/rule_engine.py
from enum import Enum
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
from datetime import datetime

class RuleCategory(Enum):
    BUDGETING = "budgeting"
    INVESTING = "investing"
    DEBT = "debt"
    RISK = "risk"
    RETIREMENT = "retirement"

@dataclass
class FinancialState:
    monthly_income: float
    monthly_expenses: float
    total_debt: float
    emergency_fund_balance: float
    investment_portfolio: float
    age: int
    risk_tolerance: str  # 'low', 'moderate', 'high'
    employment_status: str
    debt_to_income_ratio: float

class RuleEngine:
    def __init__(self, state: FinancialState):
        self.state = state
        
    def get_active_rules(self) -> Dict[RuleCategory, str]:
        """Determine which rules apply based on current financial state."""
        active = {}
        
        # Budgeting rule selection
        if self.state.emergency_fund_balance < self.state.monthly_expenses * 3:
            active[RuleCategory.BUDGETING] = "pay_yourself_first"
        elif self.state.total_debt > 0:
            active[RuleCategory.BUDGETING] = "zero_based_budgeting"
        elif self.state.monthly_income < 5000:
            active[RuleCategory.BUDGETING] = "50_30_20"
        else:
            active[RuleCategory.BUDGETING] = "60_40"
        
        # Investing rule selection
        if self.state.age > 50:
            active[RuleCategory.INVESTING] = "100_minus_age"
        elif self.state.investment_portfolio > 100000:
            active[RuleCategory.INVESTING] = "10_90_yale"
        elif self.state.risk_tolerance == "low":
            active[RuleCategory.INVESTING] = "60_40"
        else:
            active[RuleCategory.INVESTING] = "core_satellite"
        
        # Debt rule selection
        if self.state.total_debt > 0:
            if self.state.debt_to_income_ratio > 0.3:
                active[RuleCategory.DEBT] = "debt_avalanche"
            else:
                active[RuleCategory.DEBT] = "debt_snowball"
        
        return active
    
    def calculate_allocation(self, available_capital: float) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Calculate capital allocation based on active investing rule."""
        active_rules = self.get_active_rules()
        investing_rule = active_rules.get(RuleCategory.INVESTING, "core_satellite")
        
        allocations = {
            "100_minus_age": lambda: {
                "stocks": available_capital * ((100 - self.state.age) / 100),
                "bonds": available_capital * (self.state.age / 100)
            },
            "120_minus_age": lambda: {
                "stocks": available_capital * ((120 - self.state.age) / 100),
                "bonds": available_capital * ((self.state.age - 20) / 100)
            },
            "60_40": lambda: {
                "stocks": available_capital * 0.6,
                "bonds": available_capital * 0.4
            },
            "10_90_yale": lambda: {
                "traditional": available_capital * 0.1,
                "alternatives": available_capital * 0.9
            },
            "core_satellite": lambda: {
                "core_etfs": available_capital * 0.8,
                "satellite": available_capital * 0.2
            }
        }
        
        return allocations.get(investing_rule, allocations["core_satellite"])()
🔄 Part 3: Integration with Opportunity Scanner
The rule engine works in concert with the opportunity scanner to route capital intelligently.

python
# orchestrator/autopilot.py
class AutonomousWealthEngine:
    def __init__(self, state: FinancialState, duckdb_conn, rule_engine: RuleEngine):
        self.state = state
        self.conn = duckdb_conn
        self.rule_engine = rule_engine
        self.scanner = OpportunityScanner(duckdb_conn)
        
    def execute_cycle(self):
        """Run one complete autonomous wealth generation cycle."""
        active_rules = self.rule_engine.get_active_rules()
        
        # Calculate available capital based on budgeting rule
        budget_rule = active_rules[RuleCategory.BUDGETING]
        available_capital = self._calculate_surplus(budget_rule)
        
        # Get investment allocation
        allocation = self.rule_engine.calculate_allocation(available_capital)
        
        # Scan opportunities matching each allocation category
        executed_trades = []
        for category, amount in allocation.items():
            opportunities = self.scanner.scan_opportunities(
                amount, 
                CapitalTier.MICRO if amount < 500 else CapitalTier.SMALL,
                category=category
            )
            if opportunities:
                trade = self._execute_opportunity(opportunities[0], amount)
                executed_trades.append(trade)
        
        return {
            "active_rules": {k.value: v for k, v in active_rules.items()},
            "allocated": allocation,
            "executed": executed_trades,
            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
        }
    
    def _calculate_surplus(self, budget_rule: str) -> float:
        """Calculate available capital based on budgeting rule."""
        income = self.state.monthly_income
        expenses = self.state.monthly_expenses
        
        if budget_rule == "pay_yourself_first":
            return income * 0.2  # Save 20% first
        elif budget_rule == "50_30_20":
            return income * 0.2  # 20% to savings
        elif budget_rule == "60_40":
            return income * 0.4  # 40% to savings
        elif budget_rule == "zero_based_budgeting":
            return income - expenses  # All surplus
        return income * 0.2  # Default

# orchestrator/rule_activation.py
def get_optimal_budget_rule(state: FinancialState) -> str:
    if state.emergency_fund_balance < state.monthly_expenses * 3:
        return "pay_yourself_first"  # Priority: build safety net
    if state.total_debt > 5000 and state.debt_to_income_ratio > 0.2:
        return "zero_based_budgeting"  # Aggressive debt payoff
    if state.monthly_income > 7000:
        return "60_40"  # High income, aggressive saving
    return "50_30_20"  # Balanced default

def get_optimal_investing_rule(state: FinancialState, market_regime: str) -> str:
    if state.age > 55:
        return "100_minus_age"  # Capital preservation
    if state.investment_portfolio > 250000 and state.risk_tolerance == "high":
        return "10_90_yale"  # Sophisticated alternatives
    if market_regime == "high_volatility":
        return "all_weather"  # Protection in turbulent markets
    if market_regime == "high_inflation":
        return "real_assets"  # Commodities, TIPS, real estate
    return "core_satellite"  # Default optimal

def get_optimal_debt_rule(state: FinancialState) -> str:
    high_interest_debts = [d for d in state.debts if d.interest_rate > 10]
    if high_interest_debts:
        return "debt_avalanche"  # Mathematical optimization
    return "debt_snowball"  # Psychological wins for smaller debts

1.2 The Zero-Waste Rule Engine
python
# orchestrator/zero_waste_engine.py
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Dict, Optional
from enum import Enum
import asyncio

class AssetFragmentType(Enum):
    CEX_DUST = "cex_dust"
    DEX_DUST = "dex_dust"
    IDLE_CASH = "idle_cash"
    FRACTIONAL_REMAINDER = "fractional_remainder"
    SPARE_CHANGE = "spare_change"
    UNCLAIMED_REWARDS = "unclaimed_rewards"
    DEFI_DUST = "defi_dust"

@dataclass
class AssetFragment:
    fragment_type: AssetFragmentType
    source: str  # e.g., "Binance", "MetaMask", "Monzo"
    asset: str   # e.g., "TRX", "USDC", "GBP"
    amount: float
    usd_value: float
    consolidation_method: str
    target_asset: str
    gas_cost_estimate: Optional[float] = None

class ZeroWasteEngine:
    def __init__(self, duckdb_conn, rule_engine, opportunity_scanner):
        self.conn = duckdb_conn
        self.rule_engine = rule_engine
        self.scanner = opportunity_scanner
        
    async def scan_all_fragments(self) -> List[AssetFragment]:
        """Scan all connected accounts for idle value."""
        fragments = []
        fragments.extend(await self._scan_cex_dust())
        fragments.extend(await self._scan_dex_wallets())
        fragments.extend(await self._scan_idle_cash())
        fragments.extend(await self._scan_fractional_remainders())
        fragments.extend(await self._scan_unclaimed_rewards())
        return fragments
    
    async def _scan_cex_dust(self) -> List[AssetFragment]:
        """Scan Binance and other CEXs for dust balances."""
        fragments = []
        # Binance dust scanning
        binance_balances = await self._get_binance_balances()
        for asset, balance in binance_balances.items():
            if self._is_dust(asset, balance):
                usd_value = await self._get_usd_value(asset, balance)
                if usd_value > 0.50:  # Only consolidate if worth > $0.50
                    fragments.append(AssetFragment(
                        fragment_type=AssetFragmentType.CEX_DUST,
                        source="Binance",
                        asset=asset,
                        amount=balance,
                        usd_value=usd_value,
                        consolidation_method="dust_to_bnb",
                        target_asset="BNB"
                    ))
        return fragments
    
    def _is_dust(self, asset: str, balance: float) -> bool:
        """Determine if a balance qualifies as dust."""
        # Minimum trade amounts vary by asset
        min_trade_amounts = {
            "BTC": 0.0001, "ETH": 0.001, "BNB": 0.01,
            "USDT": 10, "USDC": 10, "XRP": 1, "ADA": 1,
        }
        return balance < min_trade_amounts.get(asset, 1.0)
    
    async def execute_consolidation(self, fragments: List[AssetFragment]) -> Dict:
        """Execute consolidation strategies for all fragments."""
        results = {"consolidated": [], "skipped": [], "errors": []}
        
        # Group by consolidation method for efficiency
        by_method = {}
        for f in fragments:
            method = f.consolidation_method
            if method not in by_method:
                by_method[method] = []
            by_method[method].append(f)
        
        # Execute each method
        for method, frags in by_method.items():
            if method == "dust_to_bnb":
                result = await self._execute_binance_dust_conversion(frags)
            elif method == "eip7702_batch_swap":
                result = await self._execute_eip7702_batch_swap(frags)
            elif method == "sweep_idle_cash":
                result = await self._sweep_idle_cash(frags)
            elif method == "claim_rewards":
                result = await self._claim_and_consolidate_rewards(frags)
            else:
                result = {"skipped": frags}
            
            results["consolidated"].extend(result.get("consolidated", []))
            results["skipped"].extend(result.get("skipped", []))
            results["errors"].extend(result.get("errors", []))
        
        return results
    
    async def _execute_binance_dust_conversion(self, fragments: List[AssetFragment]) -> Dict:
        """Convert Binance dust to BNB via API."""
        assets = [f.asset for f in fragments]
        # Binance dust transfer endpoint: POST /sapi/v1/asset/dust
        # Note: API currently only supports BNB as target[reference:0]
        response = await self._binance_request(
            "POST", "/sapi/v1/asset/dust",
            params={"asset": ",".join(assets)}
        )
        return {"consolidated": fragments, "response": response}
    
    async def _execute_eip7702_batch_swap(self, fragments: List[AssetFragment]) -> Dict:
        """Execute batch swap of multiple ERC-20 tokens via EIP-7702."""
        # Token Sweeper reference implementation[reference:1]
        # This requires integration with a DEX aggregator like 0x or 1inch
        tokens = [{"address": self._get_token_address(f.asset), "amount": f.amount} 
                  for f in fragments]
        # Batch swap to USDC on Base or Optimism
        result = await self._dex_aggregator.batch_swap(
            tokens=tokens,
            target_token="USDC",
            chain="base"  # or "optimism"
        )
        return {"consolidated": fragments, "tx_hash": result.get("tx_hash")}
🔄 Part 2: Binance Dust API Integration
2.1 Binance Dust Conversion Implementation
python
# connectors/binance_dust.py
import hmac
import hashlib
import time
import requests
from typing import List, Dict, Optional

class BinanceDustManager:
    def __init__(self, api_key: str, secret_key: str):
        self.api_key = api_key
        self.secret_key = secret_key
        self.base_url = "https://api.binance.com"
    
    def _sign_request(self, params: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Sign Binance API request."""
        query_string = "&".join([f"{k}={v}" for k, v in params.items()])
        signature = hmac.new(
            self.secret_key.encode('utf-8'),
            query_string.encode('utf-8'),
            hashlib.sha256
        ).hexdigest()
        params['signature'] = signature
        return params
    
    def get_dustable_assets(self) -> List[str]:
        """Get list of assets that can be converted to BNB."""
        # POST /sapi/v1/asset/dust-btc
        endpoint = "/sapi/v1/asset/dust-btc"
        timestamp = int(time.time() * 1000)
        params = self._sign_request({"timestamp": timestamp})
        response = requests.post(
            f"{self.base_url}{endpoint}",
            headers={"X-MBX-APIKEY": self.api_key},
            data=params
        )
        data = response.json()
        return [item['asset'] for item in data.get('details', [])]
    
    def convert_dust_to_bnb(self, assets: Optional[List[str]] = None) -> Dict:
        """Convert dust to BNB."""
        endpoint = "/sapi/v1/asset/dust"
        timestamp = int(time.time() * 1000)
        params = {"timestamp": timestamp}
        if assets:
            params['asset'] = ",".join(assets)
        params = self._sign_request(params)
        response = requests.post(
            f"{self.base_url}{endpoint}",
            headers={"X-MBX-APIKEY": self.api_key},
            data=params
        )
        return response.json()
    
    def get_dust_conversion_history(self) -> List[Dict]:
        """Get dust conversion history."""
        endpoint = "/sapi/v1/asset/dribblet"
        timestamp = int(time.time() * 1000)
        params = self._sign_request({"timestamp": timestamp})
        response = requests.get(
            f"{self.base_url}{endpoint}",
            headers={"X-MBX-APIKEY": self.api_key},
            params=params
        )
        data = response.json()
        # Note: API doesn't return toAsset field; need to infer from context[reference:2]
        return data.get('userAssetDribblets', [])
2.2 Multi-Exchange Dust Sweeping
python
# connectors/multi_exchange_dust.py
class MultiExchangeDustSweeper:
    def __init__(self):
        self.exchanges = {
            "binance": BinanceDustManager(api_key, secret_key),
            "bitget": BitgetDustManager(api_key, secret_passphrase),
            "kraken": KrakenDustManager(api_key, secret_key),
            "coinbase": CoinbaseDustManager(api_key, secret_key),
        }
    
    async def sweep_all_exchanges(self) -> Dict:
        """Sweep dust from all connected exchanges."""
        results = {}
        total_value = 0.0
        
        for name, manager in self.exchanges.items():
            try:
                # Get dustable assets
                dustable = manager.get_dustable_assets()
                if dustable:
                    # Convert to base asset
                    conversion = manager.convert_dust(dustable)
                    # Route to optimal yield
                    converted_amount = conversion.get('totalTransferedAmount', 0)
                    if converted_amount > 0:
                        await self._route_converted_funds(name, converted_amount)
                        total_value += converted_amount
                    results[name] = {"status": "success", "converted": converted_amount}
                else:
                    results[name] = {"status": "no_dust", "converted": 0}
            except Exception as e:
                results[name] = {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}
        
        return {"exchanges": results, "total_converted_value": total_value}
🦊 Part 3: DEX Wallet Dust Sweeping (EIP-7702)
3.1 On-Chain Dust Detection and Batch Swap
python
# connectors/dex_dust_sweeper.py
from web3 import Web3
from typing import List, Dict, Tuple

class DEXDustSweeper:
    def __init__(self, rpc_url: str, private_key: str):
        self.w3 = Web3(Web3.HTTPProvider(rpc_url))
        self.account = self.w3.eth.account.from_key(private_key)
        self.zero_x_api = "https://api.0x.org"
    
    async def scan_wallet_dust(self, wallet_address: str) -> List[Dict]:
        """Scan wallet for dust token balances."""
        # Use Covalent or Moralis API for comprehensive token discovery
        tokens = await self._get_all_token_balances(wallet_address)
        dust = []
        for token in tokens:
            usd_value = await self._get_token_usd_value(token['address'], token['balance'])
            if 0.50 < usd_value < 50:  # Dust threshold: $0.50 - $50
                dust.append({
                    "token": token['address'],
                    "symbol": token['symbol'],
                    "amount": token['balance'],
                    "usd_value": usd_value
                })
        return dust
    
    async def batch_swap_to_usdc(self, dust_tokens: List[Dict], chain_id: int = 8453) -> Dict:
        """Batch swap multiple dust tokens to USDC using 0x API."""
        if not dust_tokens:
            return {"status": "no_dust", "tx_hash": None}
        
        # Prepare batch swap via 0x API
        sell_tokens = []
        for token in dust_tokens:
            # Approve token spending first
            await self._approve_token(token['token'], token['amount'])
            sell_tokens.append({
                "sellToken": token['token'],
                "sellAmount": str(token['amount'])
            })
        
        # 0x API batch swap (if supported) or sequential swaps
        tx_hashes = []
        total_usdc_received = 0.0
        
        for token in dust_tokens:
            quote = await self._get_swap_quote(
                sell_token=token['token'],
                buy_token="0x833589fCD6eDb6E08f4c7C32D4f71b54bdA02913",  # USDC on Base
                sell_amount=token['amount'],
                chain_id=chain_id
            )
            if quote and quote.get('buyAmount'):
                tx = await self._execute_swap(quote)
                tx_hashes.append(tx)
                total_usdc_received += float(quote['buyAmount']) / 1e6
        
        return {
            "status": "success",
            "tx_hashes": tx_hashes,
            "total_usdc_received": total_usdc_received
        }
💰 Part 4: Fiat Micro-Asset Sweeping
4.1 Idle Cash Detection and Auto-Sweep
python
# connectors/fiat_micro_sweeper.py
class FiatMicroSweeper:
    def __init__(self, open_banking_connector):
        self.obc = open_banking_connector
        self.sweep_rules = {
            "Monzo": {"min_balance": 500, "sweep_to": "Trading212", "keep": 200},
            "Santander": {"min_balance": 100, "sweep_to": "PremiumBonds", "keep": 50},
            "Trading212_free_cash": {"min_balance": 50, "sweep_to": "MMF", "keep": 10},
        }
    
    async def scan_idle_cash(self) -> Dict:
        """Scan all connected accounts for idle cash."""
        idle_cash = {}
        accounts = await self.obc.get_all_accounts()
        
        for account in accounts:
            balance = account['balance']
            rule = self.sweep_rules.get(account['provider'], {})
            min_balance = rule.get('min_balance', 100)
            keep = rule.get('keep', 50)
            
            if balance > min_balance:
                sweepable = balance - keep
                idle_cash[account['id']] = {
                    "provider": account['provider'],
                    "current_balance": balance,
                    "sweepable_amount": sweepable,
                    "sweep_to": rule.get('sweep_to', 'HighYieldSavings')
                }
        
        return idle_cash
    
    async def execute_sweep(self, idle_cash: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Execute sweep of idle cash to optimal destinations."""
        results = []
        for account_id, details in idle_cash.items():
            if details['sweepable_amount'] <= 0:
                continue
            
            # Route based on destination
            if details['sweep_to'] == 'Trading212':
                result = await self._transfer_to_trading212(account_id, details['sweepable_amount'])
            elif details['sweep_to'] == 'PremiumBonds':
                result = await self._purchase_premium_bonds(details['sweepable_amount'])
            elif details['sweep_to'] == 'MMF':
                result = await self._invest_in_money_market_fund(details['sweepable_amount'])
            else:
                result = await self._transfer_to_high_yield_savings(account_id, details['sweepable_amount'])
            
            results.append(result)
        
        return {"sweeps": results, "total_swept": sum(r.get('amount', 0) for r in results)}
4.2 Spare Change Round-Up Integration
python
# connectors/spare_change_engine.py
class SpareChangeEngine:
    def __init__(self):
        self.round_up_providers = {
            "Moneybox": {"api": None, "enabled": True},
            "Plum": {"api": None, "enabled": True},
            "Trading212": {"api": None, "enabled": True, "feature": "AutoInvest"},
        }
    
    async def process_daily_roundups(self, transactions: List[Dict]) -> Dict:
        """Process daily transactions and route round-ups."""
        total_roundups = 0.0
        
        for tx in transactions:
            if tx['amount'] > 0:  # Only round up debits
                round_up = self._calculate_round_up(tx['amount'])
                total_roundups += round_up
        
        # Route round-ups to optimal destination based on active rules
        active_rules = self.rule_engine.get_active_rules()
        if active_rules.get('investing') == 'core_satellite':
            # Route to Trading 212 AutoInvest
            await self._invest_in_trading212(total_roundups, "VWRP")
        else:
            # Route to Moneybox
            await self._transfer_to_moneybox(total_roundups)
        
        return {"roundups_processed": len(transactions), "total_invested": total_roundups}
    
    def _calculate_round_up(self, amount: float) -> float:
        """Round up to nearest pound."""
        return float(int(amount)) + 1.0 - amount
🔄 Part 5: Unclaimed Rewards Auto-Claim
5.1 Staking, Airdrop, and Cashback Reward Scanning
python
# connectors/reward_claimer.py
class RewardClaimer:
    def __init__(self):
        self.staking_platforms = {
            "Lido": self._claim_lido_rewards,
            "RocketPool": self._claim_rocketpool_rewards,
            "EigenLayer": self._claim_eigenlayer_rewards,
        }
        self.cashback_platforms = {
            "TopCashback": self._claim_topcashback,
            "Cheddar": self._claim_cheddar,
            "Quidco": self._claim_quidco,
        }
    
    async def scan_and_claim_all(self) -> Dict:
        """Scan all platforms for unclaimed rewards and claim them."""
        results = {"claimed": [], "pending": [], "errors": []}
        
        # Claim staking rewards
        for platform, claim_func in self.staking_platforms.items():
            try:
                claimed = await claim_func()
                if claimed:
                    results["claimed"].append({"platform": platform, "amount": claimed})
                    # Auto-route to highest yield
                    await self._route_rewards(claimed)
            except Exception as e:
                results["errors"].append({"platform": platform, "error": str(e)})
        
        # Claim cashback
        for platform, claim_func in self.cashback_platforms.items():
            try:
                claimed = await claim_func()
                if claimed:
                    results["claimed"].append({"platform": platform, "amount": claimed})
                    await self._route_rewards(claimed)
            except Exception as e:
                results["errors"].append({"platform": platform, "error": str(e)})
        
        return results
    
    async def _claim_lido_rewards(self) -> Optional[float]:
        """Claim Lido staking rewards."""
        # stETH rewards accrue automatically via rebasing; no claim needed
        # But can harvest by unwrapping wstETH if needed
        return None
    
    async def _route_rewards(self, amount: float):
        """Route claimed rewards to optimal yield opportunity."""
        # Query opportunity scanner for best current yield
        opportunities = self.scanner.scan_opportunities(amount, CapitalTier.MICRO)
        if opportunities:
            await self._execute_opportunity(opportunities[0], amount)
📊 Part 6: The Complete Zero-Waste Integration
6.1 Unified Zero-Waste Orchestrator
python
# orchestrator/zero_waste_orchestrator.py
class ZeroWasteOrchestrator:
    def __init__(self):
        self.dust_engine = ZeroWasteEngine()
        self.multi_exchange_sweeper = MultiExchangeDustSweeper()
        self.dex_sweeper = DEXDustSweeper()
        self.fiat_sweeper = FiatMicroSweeper()
        self.spare_change_engine = SpareChangeEngine()
        self.reward_claimer = RewardClaimer()
        self.opportunity_scanner = OpportunityScanner()
    
    async def execute_full_sweep_cycle(self) -> Dict:
        """Execute a complete zero-waste sweep cycle."""
        cycle_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
        results = {
            "cycle_id": cycle_id,
            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            "cex_dust": {},
            "dex_dust": {},
            "idle_cash": {},
            "spare_change": {},
            "rewards": {},
            "total_value_recovered": 0.0,
            "redeployed_to": []
        }
        
        # 1. Sweep CEX dust
        cex_results = await self.multi_exchange_sweeper.sweep_all_exchanges()
        results["cex_dust"] = cex_results
        results["total_value_recovered"] += cex_results.get("total_converted_value", 0)
        
        # 2. Sweep DEX wallet dust
        for wallet in self.config.wallets:
            dex_results = await self.dex_sweeper.batch_swap_to_usdc(wallet)
            results["dex_dust"][wallet['address']] = dex_results
            results["total_value_recovered"] += dex_results.get("total_usdc_received", 0)
        
        # 3. Sweep idle fiat cash
        idle_cash = await self.fiat_sweeper.scan_idle_cash()
        fiat_results = await self.fiat_sweeper.execute_sweep(idle_cash)
        results["idle_cash"] = fiat_results
        results["total_value_recovered"] += fiat_results.get("total_swept", 0)
        
        # 4. Process spare change round-ups
        transactions = await self._get_todays_transactions()
        roundup_results = await self.spare_change_engine.process_daily_roundups(transactions)
        results["spare_change"] = roundup_results
        
        # 5. Claim all unclaimed rewards
        reward_results = await self.reward_claimer.scan_and_claim_all()
        results["rewards"] = reward_results
        
        # 6. Redeploy recovered value
        if results["total_value_recovered"] > 10:  # Only redeploy if > £10
            allocation = await self._redeploy_recovered_value(results["total_value_recovered"])
            results["redeployed_to"] = allocation
        
        # 7. Log to database
        await self._log_cycle_results(results)
        
        # 8. Send Telegram summary
        await self._send_summary(results)
        
        return results
    
    async def _redeploy_recovered_value(self, amount: float) -> List[Dict]:
        """Redeploy recovered value to optimal opportunities."""
        active_rules = self.rule_engine.get_active_rules()
        allocation = self.rule_engine.calculate_allocation(amount)
        
        deployed = []
        for category, alloc_amount in allocation.items():
            opportunities = self.opportunity_scanner.scan_opportunities(
                alloc_amount, CapitalTier.MICRO, category=category
            )
            if opportunities:
                result = await self._execute_opportunity(opportunities[0], alloc_amount)
                deployed.append({"category": category, "amount": alloc_amount, "opportunity": opportunities[0].name, "result": result})
        
        return deployed
6.2 Database Schema for Zero-Waste Tracking
sql
-- zero_waste_tracking.sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS zero_waste_cycles (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    cycle_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    total_value_recovered DECIMAL(20, 8),
    cex_dust_recovered DECIMAL(20, 8),
    dex_dust_recovered DECIMAL(20, 8),
    idle_cash_swept DECIMAL(20, 8),
    rewards_claimed DECIMAL(20, 8),
    redeployed_amount DECIMAL(20, 8),
    summary JSONB
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS dust_conversions (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    cycle_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    exchange TEXT NOT NULL,
    from_asset TEXT NOT NULL,
    from_amount DECIMAL(20, 8),
    to_asset TEXT NOT NULL,
    to_amount DECIMAL(20, 8),
    fee DECIMAL(20, 8),
    tx_hash TEXT,
    timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS micro_asset_sweeps (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    cycle_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    sweep_type TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'cex_dust', 'dex_dust', 'idle_cash', 'spare_change', 'rewards'
    source TEXT NOT NULL,
    asset TEXT NOT NULL,
    amount DECIMAL(20, 8),
    usd_value DECIMAL(20, 8),
    destination TEXT NOT NULL,
    status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending',
    timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

🛠️ Part 2: Building the Core Sweep Engine
This is the central brain that orchestrates every sweep. It will be built in Rust for performance and safety, with Python bindings for integration into your existing orchestration layer.

rust
// core/sweep_engine/src/lib.rs
use pyo3::prelude::*;
use std::collections::HashMap;

#[pyclass]
pub struct UniversalSweeper {
    cex_connectors: HashMap<String, Box<dyn CexConnector>>,
    wallet_scanners: Vec<Box<dyn WalletScanner>>,
    fiat_sweepers: Vec<Box<dyn FiatSweeper>>,
    reward_claimers: Vec<Box<dyn RewardClaimer>>,
}

#[pymethods]
impl UniversalSweeper {
    #[new]
    fn new() -> Self {
        UniversalSweeper {
            cex_connectors: HashMap::new(),
            wallet_scanners: Vec::new(),
            fiat_sweepers: Vec::new(),
            reward_claimers: Vec::new(),
        }
    }

    /// Execute a full zero-waste sweep cycle across all domains
    fn execute_full_sweep_cycle(&mut self) -> PyResult<HashMap<String, f64>> {
        let mut total_recovered = HashMap::new();
        
        // 1. Sweep CEX dust
        for (exchange, connector) in &self.cex_connectors {
            let recovered = connector.sweep_dust()?;
            total_recovered.insert(format!("cex_{}", exchange), recovered);
        }
        
        // 2. Sweep DEX wallet dust
        for scanner in &self.wallet_scanners {
            let recovered = scanner.scan_and_sweep()?;
            total_recovered.insert("dex_wallets".to_string(), recovered);
        }
        
        // 3. Sweep idle fiat
        for sweeper in &self.fiat_sweepers {
            let recovered = sweeper.sweep_idle_cash()?;
            total_recovered.insert("fiat_accounts".to_string(), recovered);
        }
        
        // 4. Claim unclaimed rewards
        for claimer in &self.reward_claimers {
            let recovered = claimer.claim_all()?;
            total_recovered.insert("rewards".to_string(), recovered);
        }
        
        Ok(total_recovered)
    }
}
📡 Part 3: Open-Source Components for Every Asset Class
3.1 Centralized Exchange (CEX) Dust Sweeping
You can build a custom engine that unifies API connections to all major exchanges, taking inspiration from open-source exchange engines that include dust gas collection features.

python
# connectors/cex_sweeper.py
class CexDustSweeper:
    def __init__(self):
        self.exchanges = {
            "binance": BinanceConnector(),
            "bitget": BitgetConnector(),
            "kraken": KrakenConnector(),
            "coinbase": CoinbaseConnector(),
            "bybit": BybitConnector(),
            "gate": GateConnector(),
        }
    
    async def sweep_all(self):
        total = 0.0
        for name, connector in self.exchanges.items():
            dust = await connector.get_dust_balances()
            if dust:
                converted = await connector.convert_to_base(dust)
                total += converted
        return total
3.2 DEX Wallet Dust Sweeping with EIP-7702
This is the most sophisticated part of the sweep engine, leveraging the latest Ethereum standards for gas-efficient, batch transactions. EIP-7702 enables existing wallets to execute smart contract logic, batch approvals and swaps into one transaction, and even allows for gas sponsorship—meaning you don't need to hold ETH to consolidate your tokens.

python
# connectors/dex_sweeper.py
from web3 import Web3

class EIP7702BatchSweeper:
    """Sweep multiple ERC-20 dust tokens into a single token using EIP-7702."""
    
    def __init__(self, rpc_url: str, private_key: str):
        self.w3 = Web3(Web3.HTTPProvider(rpc_url))
        self.account = self.w3.eth.account.from_key(private_key)
    
    async def batch_sweep(self, tokens: List[str], target_token: str):
        # 1. Scan wallet for all token balances
        balances = await self._scan_balances()
        
        # 2. Filter for dust (e.g., value < $10)
        dust = {t: b for t, b in balances.items() if self._is_dust(t, b)}
        
        # 3. Execute EIP-7702 batch swap via 0x API
        tx_hash = await self._execute_batch_swap(dust, target_token)
        
        return tx_hash
You can also take inspiration from projects like DUST.OPS (a cross-chain token sweeper with optional privacy routing) and Dust.fun (which consolidates low-value tokens across multiple chains into a single asset).

1.2 Role-Based Access Control for Shared Portfolios
python
# orchestrator/rbac.py
from enum import Enum
from typing import List, Optional
from pydantic import BaseModel

class Role(Enum):
    OWNER = "owner"           # Full control
    ADMIN = "admin"           # Can manage users but not delete
    PARTNER = "partner"       # View + edit + trade
    VIEWER = "viewer"         # View only
    RESTRICTED = "restricted" # View specific portfolios only

class PortfolioPermission(BaseModel):
    portfolio_id: str
    user_id: str
    role: Role
    can_trade: bool = False
    can_withdraw: bool = False
    view_sensitive: bool = False  # Hide exact amounts, show percentages only

class RBACManager:
    def __init__(self, db_conn):
        self.conn = db_conn
    
    async def check_permission(self, user_id: str, portfolio_id: str, action: str) -> bool:
        """Check if user has permission for action on portfolio."""
        result = self.conn.execute("""
            SELECT role, can_trade, can_withdraw, view_sensitive 
            FROM portfolio_permissions 
            WHERE user_id = ? AND portfolio_id = ?
        """, [user_id, portfolio_id]).fetchone()
        
        if not result:
            return False
        
        role, can_trade, can_withdraw, view_sensitive = result
        
        if action == "view":
            return True
        elif action == "trade":
            return can_trade or role in [Role.OWNER.value, Role.ADMIN.value]
        elif action == "withdraw":
            return can_withdraw or role == Role.OWNER.value
        elif action == "admin":
            return role in [Role.OWNER.value, Role.ADMIN.value]
        
        return False
1.3 Shared Portfolio Views with Activity Feed
sql
-- shared_activity_feed.sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS shared_portfolios (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    owner_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
    name TEXT NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS portfolio_members (
    portfolio_id UUID REFERENCES shared_portfolios(id),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    role TEXT NOT NULL,
    joined_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    PRIMARY KEY (portfolio_id, user_id)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS activity_feed (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    portfolio_id UUID REFERENCES shared_portfolios(id),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    action TEXT NOT NULL,
    details JSONB,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Index for fast feed retrieval
CREATE INDEX idx_activity_feed_portfolio ON activity_feed(portfolio_id, created_at DESC);

dart
// lib/services/biometric_service.dart
import 'package:local_auth/local_auth.dart';

class BiometricService {
  final LocalAuthentication _auth = LocalAuthentication();
  
  Future<bool> authenticate() async {
    try {
      return await _auth.authenticate(
        localizedReason: 'Authenticate to access Financial OS',
        options: const AuthenticationOptions(
          stickyAuth: true,
          biometricOnly: true,
        ),
      );
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }
  
  Future<bool> isBiometricAvailable() async {
    return await _auth.canCheckBiometrics;
  }
}

3.2 Receipt Processing Pipeline
python
# services/receipt_processor.py
import pytesseract
from PIL import Image
import requests
from typing import Dict, Optional

class ReceiptProcessor:
    def __init__(self, ollama_url: str = "http://ollama:11434"):
        self.ollama_url = ollama_url
    
    async def process_receipt(self, image_path: str) -> Dict:
        # 1. OCR extraction
        image = Image.open(image_path)
        text = pytesseract.image_to_string(image)
        
        # 2. LLM categorization
        prompt = f"""Extract the following from this receipt text:
        - Merchant name
        - Total amount
        - Date
        - Category (one of: groceries, dining, transportation, shopping, entertainment, utilities, healthcare, other)
        - List of line items with names and prices
        
        Receipt text: {text}
        
        Respond in JSON format."""
        
        response = requests.post(
            f"{self.ollama_url}/api/generate",
            json={"model": "llama3.2:3b", "prompt": prompt, "stream": False}
        )
        
        return response.json()
    
    async def auto_categorize_and_log(self, receipt_data: Dict, user_id: str):
        """Auto-categorize and log expense to Actual Budget."""
        category = receipt_data.get('category', 'other')
        amount = receipt_data.get('total_amount', 0)
        merchant = receipt_data.get('merchant', 'Unknown')
        
        # Log to Actual Budget via API
        await self._log_to_actual_budget(user_id, merchant, amount, category)
💳 Part 4: Subscription Optimization & Bill Negotiation
4.1 Subscription Detection from Bank Statements
python
# services/subscription_detector.py
import re
from typing import List, Dict
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

class SubscriptionDetector:
    def __init__(self, duckdb_conn):
        self.conn = duckdb_conn
        self.known_subscriptions = {
            "Netflix": ["netflix.com", "NETFLIX"],
            "Spotify": ["spotify.com", "SPOTIFY"],
            "Amazon Prime": ["amazon prime", "PRIME"],
            "Disney+": ["disneyplus.com", "DISNEY+"],
            "Apple": ["apple.com/bill", "APPLE.COM/BILL"],
            "Adobe": ["adobe.com", "ADOBE"],
            "Microsoft": ["microsoft.com", "MICROSOFT*"],
            "Google": ["google storage", "GOOGLE*"],
        }
    
    async def scan_for_subscriptions(self, user_id: str) -> List[Dict]:
        """Scan last 3 months of transactions for recurring payments."""
        three_months_ago = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=90)
        
        transactions = self.conn.execute("""
            SELECT description, amount, date 
            FROM pg_db.transactions 
            WHERE user_id = ? AND date >= ? AND amount < 0
            ORDER BY date DESC
        """, [user_id, three_months_ago]).fetchdf()
        
        subscriptions = []
        for merchant, patterns in self.known_subscriptions.items():
            merchant_txs = transactions[
                transactions['description'].str.contains('|'.join(patterns), case=False, na=False)
            ]
            if len(merchant_txs) >= 2:  # At least 2 occurrences
                avg_amount = merchant_txs['amount'].mean()
                last_date = merchant_txs['date'].max()
                subscriptions.append({
                    "merchant": merchant,
                    "monthly_cost": abs(avg_amount),
                    "last_charged": last_date,
                    "occurrences": len(merchant_txs)
                })
        
        return subscriptions
4.2 Bill Negotiation Alerts
python
# services/bill_negotiator.py
class BillNegotiator:
    def __init__(self):
        self.negotiable_bills = {
            "internet": ["Plusnet", "BT", "Virgin Media", "Sky", "TalkTalk"],
            "mobile": ["EE", "Vodafone", "O2", "Three", "Giffgaff"],
            "insurance": ["Admiral", "Aviva", "Direct Line", "LV=", "AXA"],
            "energy": ["British Gas", "E.ON", "EDF", "Scottish Power", "Octopus"],
        }
    
    async def check_negotiation_opportunities(self, user_id: str) -> List[Dict]:
        """Identify bills that could be negotiated."""
        subscriptions = await self.subscription_detector.scan_for_subscriptions(user_id)
        
        opportunities = []
        for sub in subscriptions:
            for category, providers in self.negotiable_bills.items():
                if any(p.lower() in sub['merchant'].lower() for p in providers):
                    # Check if bill is above market rate
                    market_rate = self._get_market_rate(category)
                    if sub['monthly_cost'] > market_rate * 1.2:  # 20% above market
                        opportunities.append({
                            "merchant": sub['merchant'],
                            "current_cost": sub['monthly_cost'],
                            "market_rate": market_rate,
                            "potential_savings": sub['monthly_cost'] - market_rate,
                            "category": category,
                            "negotiation_script": self._generate_script(sub['merchant'], sub['monthly_cost'], market_rate)
                        })
        
        return opportunities
    
    def _generate_script(self, merchant: str, current: float, target: float) -> str:
        return f"""Call {merchant} and say:
"I've been a loyal customer for [X] years, but I've found a comparable deal for £{target:.2f}/month. 
Can you match this rate to keep my business?"
Expected savings: £{current - target:.2f}/month (£{(current - target) * 12:.2f}/year)"""
📊 Part 5: Real Estate & Alternative Asset Valuation
5.1 Property Value Auto-Updates via Zoopla/Rightmove
python
# services/property_valuation.py
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

class PropertyValuation:
    def __init__(self):
        self.zoopla_api_key = os.getenv("ZOOPLA_API_KEY")
    
    async def get_estimated_value(self, postcode: str, property_type: str = "house") -> Dict:
        """Get estimated property value from Zoopla API."""
        # Zoopla API endpoint
        url = "https://api.zoopla.co.uk/api/v1/property/richlist"
        params = {
            "api_key": self.zoopla_api_key,
            "area": postcode,
            "output_type": "outcode"
        }
        response = requests.get(url, params=params)
        data = response.json()
        
        if data.get('average_values'):
            return {
                "postcode": postcode,
                "estimated_value": data['average_values'].get('average_price', 0),
                "confidence": "medium"
            }
        
        # Fallback to scraping if API unavailable
        return await self._scrape_valuation(postcode)
    
    async def update_portfolio_properties(self, user_id: str):
        """Update all properties in user's portfolio."""
        properties = self.conn.execute("""
            SELECT id, postcode, property_type, last_valuation, last_updated
            FROM pg_db.properties WHERE user_id = ?
        """, [user_id]).fetchdf()
        
        for _, prop in properties.iterrows():
            valuation = await self.get_estimated_value(prop['postcode'], prop['property_type'])
            self.conn.execute("""
                UPDATE pg_db.properties 
                SET current_value = ?, last_valuation = NOW()
                WHERE id = ?
            """, [valuation['estimated_value'], prop['id']])
📈 Part 6: Credit Score Monitoring Integration
6.1 Unified Credit Score Dashboard
python
# services/credit_monitor.py
import requests
from typing import Dict, List

class CreditMonitor:
    def __init__(self):
        self.providers = {
            "clearscore": ClearScoreConnector(),
            "creditkarma": CreditKarmaConnector(),
            "experian": ExperianConnector(),  # via MSE Credit Club
        }
    
    async def get_all_scores(self, user_id: str) -> Dict:
        """Fetch credit scores from all connected providers."""
        scores = {}
        for name, connector in self.providers.items():
            try:
                score = await connector.get_score(user_id)
                scores[name] = score
            except Exception as e:
                scores[name] = {"error": str(e)}
        
        return scores
    
    async def get_credit_improvement_tips(self, scores: Dict) -> List[str]:
        """Generate actionable credit improvement tips."""
        tips = []
        avg_score = sum(s.get('score', 0) for s in scores.values() if 'score' in s) / len(scores)
        
        if avg_score < 560:
            tips.append("Register on electoral roll at your current address")
            tips.append("Use credit builder card for small purchases, pay in full monthly")
        elif avg_score < 720:
            tips.append("Keep credit utilization below 25%")
            tips.append("Avoid multiple credit applications in short period")
        else:
            tips.append("Maintain current good habits")
            tips.append("Consider increasing credit limit to lower utilization ratio")
        
        return tips
🏛️ Part 7: Automated Tax Filing & Compliance
7.1 HMRC API Integration for Self Assessment
python
# compliance/hmrc_filer.py
import requests
from datetime import datetime
import json

class HMRCSelfAssessmentFiler:
    def __init__(self, client_id: str, client_secret: str):
        self.client_id = client_id
        self.client_secret = client_secret
        self.base_url = "https://api.service.hmrc.gov.uk"
        self.token = None
    
    async def authenticate(self):
        """OAuth2 authentication with HMRC."""
        response = requests.post(
            f"{self.base_url}/oauth/token",
            data={
                "grant_type": "client_credentials",
                "client_id": self.client_id,
                "client_secret": self.client_secret,
                "scope": "read:vat write:vat read:self-assessment write:self-assessment"
            }
        )
        self.token = response.json()['access_token']
    
    async def submit_self_assessment(self, tax_year: str, return_data: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Submit Self Assessment return directly to HMRC."""
        if not self.token:
            await self.authenticate()
        
        response = requests.post(
            f"{self.base_url}/individuals/self-assessment/return/{tax_year}",
            headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {self.token}"},
            json=return_data
        )
        return response.json()
    
    async def get_tax_calculation(self, income: float, gains: float, dividends: float, tax_year: str) -> Dict:
        """Calculate estimated tax liability."""
        # 2026/27 rates
        personal_allowance = 12570
        basic_rate_limit = 37700
        
        total_income = income + gains + dividends
        taxable = max(0, total_income - personal_allowance)
        
        income_tax = min(taxable, basic_rate_limit) * 0.20
        if taxable > basic_rate_limit:
            income_tax += (taxable - basic_rate_limit) * 0.40
        
        cgt_allowance = 3000
        taxable_gains = max(0, gains - cgt_allowance)
        cgt = taxable_gains * 0.14  # Basic rate
        
        dividend_allowance = 500
        taxable_divs = max(0, dividends - dividend_allowance)
        dividend_tax = taxable_divs * 0.1075  # Basic rate
        
        return {
            "income_tax": income_tax,
            "capital_gains_tax": cgt,
            "dividend_tax": dividend_tax,
            "total_tax_due": income_tax + cgt + dividend_tax,
            "tax_year": tax_year
        }
7.2 MTD Quarterly Submission Automation
python
# compliance/mtd_bridge.py
class MTDBridge:
    def __init__(self, hmrc_filer: HMRCSelfAssessmentFiler):
        self.filer = hmrc_filer
    
    async def submit_quarterly_update(self, vat_number: str, period_start: str, period_end: str) -> Dict:
        """Submit quarterly MTD VAT return."""
        # Calculate VAT obligations from Actual Budget data
        vat_data = await self._calculate_vat_obligations(period_start, period_end)
        
        payload = {
            "periodKey": f"{period_start[:7]}",
            "vatDueSales": vat_data['vat_due_sales'],
            "vatDueAcquisitions": vat_data['vat_due_acquisitions'],
            "totalVatDue": vat_data['total_vat_due'],
            "vatReclaimedCurrPeriod": vat_data['vat_reclaimed'],
            "netVatDue": vat_data['net_vat_due'],
            "totalValueSalesExVAT": vat_data['total_sales'],
            "totalValuePurchasesExVAT": vat_data['total_purchases'],
        }
        
        response = requests.post(
            f"{self.filer.base_url}/organisations/vat/{vat_number}/returns",
            headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {self.filer.token}"},
            json=payload
        )
        return response.json()
